	if test -d `pwd`/../tools/ioemu-qemu-xen; then \

	else \
		if [ ! -d ioemu-remote ]; then \
			rm -rf ioemu-remote ioemu-remote.tmp; \
			mkdir ioemu-remote.tmp; rmdir ioemu-remote.tmp; \
			git clone `pwd`/../tools/ioemu-qemu-xen ioemu-remote.tmp; \
			if [ "xen-4.1.1" ]; then			\
				cd ioemu-remote.tmp;			\

			mv ioemu-remote.tmp ioemu-remote; \
		fi; \
		rm -f ioemu-dir; \
